          (norm): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
        (conv3): Conv2d(
          512, 2048, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(2048, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
      (1): BottleneckBlock(
        (conv1): Conv2d(
          2048, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
        (conv2): Conv2d(
          512, 512, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
        (conv3): Conv2d(
          512, 2048, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(2048, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
      (2): BottleneckBlock(
        (conv1): Conv2d(
          2048, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
        (conv2): Conv2d(
          512, 512, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
        (conv3): Conv2d(
          512, 2048, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False
          (norm): BatchNorm2d(2048, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
    )
    (box_predictor): FastRCNNOutputLayers(
      (cls_score): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=81, bias=True)
      (bbox_pred): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=320, bias=True)
    )
  )
)
